We arrived early and there was a buzz in the church as many of the parishioners were visiting with each other. That‚Äôs fine and all as it builds community, but they didn‚Äôt even try to keep it somewhat quiet for those coming early and wanting some quiet to prepare their hearts for the Word and Communion. The buzz increased as more people arrived, and it was more like we were at the theatre than in a worship space. It finally quieted down, but the congregation never seemed to settle into Mass. There was lots going on between pews, and I don‚Äôt mean just the understandable fussy children, but likewise inattentive adults. <Rating>5<//Rating><text>I had my doubts about attending mass in Beverly Hills, I didn't want to deal with stuck up people and all the stereotypes the rich have, but I gave it a chance. From the moment I first set foot in the church I truely felt like I was coming home. We have no other family in the area and The Church of the Good Shepherd is where I feel like I am welcome, accepted and wanted. My family has nothing in common with other people in the parish, other than being Catholic, but I don't feel any of that at the church or the socials we have attended. We have tried many, many other Catholic perishes in the area, and across the country, and this is the best (other than the Church I grew up in). Father Ed's homilies are always relevant and on point. Other Priests who hold mass from time to time are also relevant and bring the readings to today and relating to everyday life. Unfortunately Father Ed and Michelle are not able to stay on top of everything at every moment right now due to a very small staff and other responsibilities in the diocese. If you attend Mass you can be sure to feel the presence of Christ and come away with some ideas and understanding of how Christ is present and working and how you can make your life more relevant to following Christ. Any negative reviews can be reconsidered by trying to be more Christ like and filling in where the church is lacking to make the community more whole. You will not be disappointed in mass or the presence of Christ at the church. Everything outside of mass at a Catholic Church is a group project and takes participation from the community, if you see a need than fill it to make it better rather than criticizing and trying to turn others away. God Bless</text><Pictures>None</Pictures><response>None</response>< gmapID>

< Review>
I called in during the week to set up a wedding date. A woman named Michelle had answered the phone and set up an appointment to meet with A Father Ed. We went in on a Saturday, my fiancee and I to meet Father Ed to set up our wedding and date and to learn more about the church experience. Needless to say 2 weeks went by and we were waiting for Father Ed to get back to us on a few SIMPLE questions. I had called in because no one was responding to us. I had gotten Michelle back on the phone inquiring about the date we set with Father Ed as well as the unanswered questions from our first meeting. Michelle took my information and instructed me that she would be speaking with Father Ed after he got in AFTER 12 and she would then circle back with me on feedback. So, TWO days later I called back again for a 3rd time, still unaware of where my fiance and I stood with our Wedding date  and our meeting with Father Ed.  Michelle now picked up the phone and said " Why are you calling!, I told you I would get back with you when I hear something.." Now 4 weeks have transpired and still no response from anyone at this point. My poor sweet fiance called in and asked if she could speak Michelle. Michelle now at this screened her call and told the gentleman through the phone she has not heard anything and why are we calling back?
I urge anyone who is looking to find a church to call home, this is not the place. If you are looking for a Priest or front parish with INTEGRITY. This is not the place to call home. STAY AWAY FROM THIS CHURCH. They are the reason our Catholic church has a bad name, people like this who are careless. I am disappointed in this place Father Ed, Michelle and those in that parish that they do not take their roles more serious. I want people everywhere to know what the experience is like in this place, a Catholic born and raised that people. This is a careless Lot. You should be ashamed to call yourself a CHRISTIAN. By the way look at the other manufactured reviews included here they have no substance. Is this church employing people to post a review in their behalf??? WOW!!
from a concerned Born and raised Catholic who has spent his entire life apart of the St. Cyrils parish</Review>

< Text>
I had high hopes for this place because of the high reviews but my experience was just average. The flavors of the food were good but the dishes were lacking. The lemon chicken was very thin sliced. So thin it was like a chicken chip with lemon dipping sauce. The Mongolian beef had very little beef and a thousand veggies. The soups were the best part of the meal. Skip the fortune cookies they tasted like cheap imitation versions. Overall it felt like they were cutting corners on the meal trying to save money. I'm not ready to give up on the restaurant just yet but I will look at others before I give them another shot . hopefully there other dishes are more impressive<//Text>

<Rating>4</Rating><Text>The appetizers served before the main course is quite bland by itself, however the sweet and sour sauce is tasty and unique. My entire meal was served to me directly and the drink I ordered, (coke), is well mixed and their smoothies, e.G. mango, strawberry, and taro, look delicious as well. The atmosphere is simple, relaxing and I have a strong feeling that when this place gets crowded, it will get hectic. I ordered the Orange chicken with the upgraded side of Chow Mein. The Chow Mein was well prepared and to go along with that the Orange Chicken was outstanding. The perfect amount of crisp tag-teaming with the perfect amount of sauce made it and outstanding dinner. The servings are larger than expected and would feed a happy couple easily. Everything is fresh made so it is hot when served and stays hot throughout the meal. I am not a fan of the plastic forks and paper cups but, I do agree with their idea on the no lid policy. The restaurant is absolutely Family Friendly. The staff is kind and serves your food to you with speed and efficiency. (Although it could change based on popularity). All in all it's cheaper than Panda Express, it tastes better than Panda Express. It has the variety of P.F. Chang's. It is an all around great place to eat. (Total was $13.10). I highly recommend to anyone who wants an upgrade to Panda Express at a cheaper price. This place is fantastic and I hope this review was resourceful.</Text>< Pics>

Absolutely, one of the most economical, reasonable portions, and extremely down to Earth servers over the counter. It's arguably one of the few places where I find great customer service, great food, and an affordable price. Whenever, I dine in to eat, I regularly order a veggie sandwich, one cookie, and iced unsweented black tea for an afforable price. < Review>
I was rear ended in early August of 2012 by a drunk driver. It was multiple car accident and the drunk driver hit two vehicles, including mine, in plain daylight and then tried to drive his car onto the sidewalk and when the car didn't move, he tried to run on foot before finally being caught by the police.

I contacted another law firm first thing on Monday morning since the accident took place over the weekend. When I reported the accident to my insurance I asked them about seeing a doctor, they simply told me to pay out of pocket and then I would be reimbursed. That to me didn't sound right since both me and my son were injured in the accident.

When I called the other law firm, based on the Yelp reviews, I was greeted by a female employee who asked me to email her the pictures from the accident and someone would contact me shortly. I emailed her the pictures on Monday around 9am. I didn't hear back from anyone that day. After work, I ended up going to Urgent Care because my back and my shoulder were killing me. I was in pain. I also took my son to get a quick check up just to make sure. Since I have a PPO, I ended up paying $40 off the back for the visits and an additional $39 in medication. $79.00 just in one visit!!!!

On Tuesday morning my shoulder, back and neck were killing me again. So, I sent a follow up email to the same staff at the other law firm with an additional video from the accident that my son had taken with his phone. I didn't get a response to either one of the emails. I went ahead and called the office in the afternoon to see if they had received any of my emails. The same staff answered the phone and advised me she had forward that information to a case manager.

At that point, I wasn't sure what to make out of it. So, I contacted Jonathan Yagoubzadeh and emailed his office the same pictures and video I had sent to other law office. Jonathan called me within 30 minutes and took the time to talk to me directly, asked the necessary questions, explained the process, and was kind enough to find a medical provider close to my office. He even offered to meet me at a convenient time and place so I wouldn't have to drive to his office to see him.

I decided to think about it since I had already contacted the other law firm. On the same day, I got a phone call from the other law firm's case manager who was very nice, but wanted to set up an appointment and for me to drive to Huntington Beach at a time that wasn't convenient. I sent up an appointment, but wasn't fully convinced since it seemed like I was the one pursuing them, doing the follow up, and I wondered if that's the way I would be treated during the whole process.

I decided to contact Jonathan again and let him handle my case, his staff met with me at a convenient time and place and the process began to roll. He also got me in to see the doctor right away and I didn't have to pay anything out of pocket. No more $20 co-payments for visits and medication. The attorney calls to check in with me and so does his case manager/legal assistant. They take the time to answer my calls, emails, and all my questions... even when I ask them twice. At times they are busy, but they are kind and professional enough to set up appointments to talk to me and answer my questions. Their follow up is amazing.

This case finally settled. The settlement process is lengthy, so be patient and know that Jonathan and his staff are taking care of you. I can't disclose the financial settlement, but lets just say it was enough for a down payment on a three bedroom house in a decent area of Long Beach, CA. Thank you for your amazing customer service and attention to details Jonathan! You and your staff made this whole process very easy and thank you for always being so patient with me (even when I asked the same question 3 times).<//Review>
